@RedSquirrel: I finally converted fluxbox-generate_menu to generate-openbox-menu.  It works fine, and has all the non-icon related options of the original.  It just has some nasty kludges in it in order to prevent the output of empty sub-menus.  I've worked out a way to elegantly remove them, but it will require rewriting most of the script...  in the mean time, I'm trying to figure out the sed-fu in the original script that handled the empty menus.

---

### Post by quirkification on 2010-07-03
> **jetsam said:**
> negotiation

Last six posts were messed up.  First letter of each word should start with the last letter of the previous word, so next word should start with 'n.'

yea this is CHAIN association, there is also just "[word association]("http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=86033&page=4742")". That is the thread where you respond to the word with a word that is inspired by the previous.

This thread is a response with a word that starts with the last letter of the word before you, so it is a chain. And if it also happens to be an associated word like the other thread, then kudos to you :D.


[SIZE="2"]Superstition[/SIZE] > [SIZE="3"]Negotiation[/SIZE] > [SIZE="4"]**Negative**[/SIZE]

@Samthorn:  this is *chain* word association, so the first letter of each word should start with the last letter of the previous word.  If the words are associated in meaning as well, then that's good but not required.

> Matroska

### Post by jetsam on 2010-07-23
> **pricetech said:**
> salamander

> **Goolie said:**
> newt

:(

Using letterman powers:  "**went**" is an anagram of "**newt**."  Change the 'w' to 'r and we have "**rent**", which is correct and leaves the next move, "**trinity**", legal.

salamander -> rent -> trinity

**yeasty**

@jerenept, this is not "_normal_" word association game, but "_chain_" word association. Please try to continue with a word starting with the last letter of the previous word, that is with a "**k**" eg...


**knighthood**

...if you can also do a "normal" association along with the "chain" association-- all the better ;).

### Post by Macskeeball on 2011-06-13
skyman

[COLOR="Silver"]This isn't the regular word association game. It's a chain. Use the last letter of the previous post to start a new word. As a mod, maybe you should edit the first post to make this more clear. Bold the d in red, the g in dog, and the d in good. But maybe change those example words so they're completely unrelated to each other except by the letter chain.[/color]
